â”‚ Now I'll structure the recommendations into 2 categories:

**Category 1: Architectural Improvements**
- Extract playback state machine (play/pause/stop logic)
- Consolidate preset definitions (eliminate duplication)
- Create unified RAF coordinator
- Implement token usage standardization
- Reduce theater component instance proliferation

**Category 2: Functionality Improvements**
- Add timeline support (currently removed)
- Add scroll-triggered animations (currently removed)
- Improve responsive API (container queries)
- Add animation composition utilities
- Performance profiler/debugger
- Add spring physics presets
- Gesture integration (drag, swipe)

These align with the agent findings and provide concrete, actionable improvements.   â”‚
